# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="f0761-105">Miembros obsoletos en .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0761-105">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f0761-106">En este artículo se enumeran los miembros de tipo que están obsoletos en .NET Framework 4.5 y versiones posteriores.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0761-106">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0761-107">Los miembros de tipo se agrupan por ensamblado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0761-107">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f0761-108">En este artículo no se muestran los miembros de los tipos obsoletos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0761-108">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0761-109">Para obtener una lista de tipos obsoletos, vea [Tipos obsoletos](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0761-109">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

## <a name="iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="f0761-1111">IEHost.dll e IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0761-1111">IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f0761-1112">Se han quitado de .NET Framework los ensamblados IEHost.dll e IEExec.exe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0761-1112">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0761-1113">Todos sus tipos y miembros están obsoletos y no se admiten en .NET Framework 4.5 y versiones posteriores.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0761-1113">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported in .NET Framework 4.5 and later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0761-1114">Estos ensamblados se utilizaban para hospedar los controles de Windows Forms y ejecutar las aplicaciones ejecutables en Internet Explorer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0761-1114">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f0761-1115">Entre las alternativas a esta tecnología están ClickOnce, Aplicaciones de explorador XAML (XBAP) y Microsoft Silverlight.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f0761-1115">Alternatives to this technology include ClickOnce, XAML Browser Applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
